2002-2005 \xd0\xb6\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b \xd0\xa5\xd1\x83 \xd0\xa6\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbd\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbe(\xd2\x9b\xd1\x8b\xd1\x82. \xe8\x83\xa1\xe9\x94\xa6\xe6\xb6\x9b) \xd3\xa9\xd0\xb7\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd\xd1\x96\xd2\xa3 \xd2\x9b\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xb6\xd0\xbe\xd2\x93\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b \xd0\xbf\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd1\x82\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd2\x9b, \xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd1\x82\xd1\x96\xd0\xba \xd0\xb6\xd3\x99\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5 \xd3\x99\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb8 \xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd1\x83\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb7\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b \xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b (\xd2\x9a\xd0\x9a\xd0\x9f \xd0\x9e\xd0\x9a \xd0\xb6\xd0\xbe\xd2\x93\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd2\x93\xd1\x8b \xd1\x82\xd3\xa9\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd2\x93\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b, \xd2\x9a\xd0\xa5\xd0\xa0 \xd0\xbf\xd1\x80\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb4\xd1\x81\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbb\xd1\x96, \xd2\x9a\xd0\xa5\xd0\x91\xd0\x90 \xd0\xb1\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81 \xd2\x9b\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb1\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd1\x88\xd1\x8b\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b).\n

\xd0\x96\xd0\x86\xd3\xa8 \xd0\xba\xd3\xa9\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd1\x96 \xd0\xb1\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb9\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd1\x88\xd0\xb0, \xd2\x9a\xd1\x8b\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9 \xd0\x90\xd2\x9a\xd0\xa8-\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd \xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb9\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb3\xd1\x96 \xd0\xb5\xd0\xba\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd\xd1\x88\xd1\x96 \xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b \xd0\xb8\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd1\x96\xd0\xbf \xd0\xb6\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b\xd1\x80[10]. \xd0\x92\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8e\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd2\x9b \xd1\x80\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb2\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd1\x96 \xd0\xb6\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbc \xd3\xa9\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x96. \xd0\xa1\xd1\x8b\xd1\x80\xd1\x82\xd2\x9b\xd1\x8b \xd1\x81\xd0\xb0\xd1\x83\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xba\xd3\xa9\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd1\x96 2004 \xd0\xb6\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd2\x93\xd0\xb0 \xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9 850 \xd0\xbc\xd0\xbb\xd1\x80\xd0\xb4 \xd0\xb4\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd \xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbf \xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd1\x82\xd1\x96.\n

2005 \xd0\xb6\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 \xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd \xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xb5\xd2\xa3 \xd1\x96\xd1\x80\xd1\x96 \xd2\xb1\xd1\x8f\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b \xd0\xb1\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd1\x81 \xd0\xbe\xd0\xbf\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 \xd2\x9b\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb7\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd \xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd1\x82\xd1\x96\xd0\xba \xd0\xb1\xd0\xb0\xd2\x9b\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd1\x83\xd2\x93\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd1\x83 \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd1\x83\xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b \xd0\xb1\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b. \xd0\x96\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbf\xd0\xbf\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9 \xd1\x81\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb1\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b\xd2\x93\xd1\x8b \xd2\xaf\xd1\x88\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd \xd0\xb6\xd0\xb8\xd1\x96 \xd1\x81\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd \xd0\x93\xd1\x83\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd1\x83\xd0\xbd \xd0\xbf\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbd\xd1\x86\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xbf\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd1\x82\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd2\x9b \xd0\xb6\xd3\x99\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd1\x82\xd1\x96\xd0\xba \xd0\xb1\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd1\x88\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd2\x9b\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b \xd1\x81\xd0\xbe\xd1\x82\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd1\x83 \xd0\xb1\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b.\n

\xd2\x9a\xd0\x9a\xd0\x9f \xd0\x9e\xd0\x9a \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd1\x83\xd0\xbc\xd1\x8b 2005 \xd0\xb6\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 \xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0 \xc2\xab\xd2\x9a\xd1\x8b\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0 \xd2\xaf\xd0\xb9\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd1\x96\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb4\xd1\x96 \xd2\x9b\xd0\xbe\xd2\x93\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b \xd2\x9b\xd2\xb1\xd1\x80\xd1\x83\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b \xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd2\x9b \xd0\xbc\xd0\xb0\xd2\x9b\xd1\x81\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82 \xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd\xc2\xbb 11-\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd\xd1\x88\xd1\x96 \xd0\xb1\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd0\xb6\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b\xd2\x9b \xd0\xb6\xd0\xbe\xd1\x81\xd0\xbf\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80 \xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb1\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b.\n

1949 \xd0\xb6\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 \xd0\xb6\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbb\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd2\x9b\xd1\x81\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0 \xd2\x9a\xd0\xa5\xd0\xa0 \xd2\x9b\xd2\xb1\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd2\x93\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b \xd0\xb5\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5 \xd1\x82\xd3\xa9\xd1\x80\xd1\x82 \xd0\x9a\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbd\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb8\xd1\x82\xd1\x83\xd1\x86\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f \xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb1\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b(1954, 1975, 1978 \xd0\xb8 1982). \xd2\x9a\xd1\x8b\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9 \xd0\xa5\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd2\x9b \xd0\xa0\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd0\xbf\xd1\x83\xd0\xb1\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb8\xd0\xba\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 \xd0\x9a\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbd\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb8\xd1\x82\xd1\x83\xd1\x86\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b \xd0\xb1\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb9\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd1\x88\xd0\xb0 (1982 \xd0\xb6\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 \xd0\xb6\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbb\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd2\x9b\xd1\x81\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b), \xd2\x9a\xd0\xa5\xd0\xa0 \xe2\x80\x94 \xd1\x85\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd2\x9b\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 \xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xbe\xd0\xba\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd2\x9b \xd3\xa9\xd0\xba\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb4\xd1\x96\xd0\xb3\xd1\x96 \xd0\xb1\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80 \xd1\x81\xd0\xbe\xd1\x86\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb8\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x96\xd0\xba \xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82.\n

\xd0\x9c\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd1\x82\xd1\x96\xd0\xba \xd0\xb1\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbb\xd1\x96\xd0\xba\xd1\x82\xd1\x96\xd2\xa3 \xd0\xb6\xd0\xbe\xd2\x93\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd2\x93\xd1\x8b \xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b \xe2\x80\x94 \xd0\xb6\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb3\xd1\x96\xd0\xbb\xd1\x96\xd0\xba\xd1\x82\xd1\x96 \xd0\xb6\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0 5 \xd0\xb6\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd2\x93\xd0\xb0 \xd1\x81\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd \xd1\x85\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd2\x9b \xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd1\x83\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd \xd1\x82\xd2\xb1\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd 2979 \xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbf\xd1\x83\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd \xd1\x82\xd2\xb1\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd \xd0\xb1\xd1\x96\xd1\x80 \xd0\xbf\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b \xd0\x91\xd2\xaf\xd0\xba\xd1\x96\xd0\xbb \xd2\x9a\xd1\x8b\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9 \xd1\x85\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd2\x9b \xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd1\x83\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 \xd0\xb6\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b (\xd0\x91\xd2\x9a\xd0\xa5\xd2\x9a\xd0\x96). \xd0\x91\xd2\x9a\xd0\xa5\xd2\x9a\xd0\x96 \xd1\x81\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd1\x81\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b \xd0\xb6\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb \xd1\x81\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd2\x93\xd1\x8b \xd1\x82\xd3\x99\xd1\x80\xd1\x82\xd1\x96\xd0\xbf\xd0\xbf\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd \xd1\x88\xd0\xb0\xd2\x9b\xd1\x8b\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b.\n

\xd0\x94\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbf\xd1\x83\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 \xd1\x81\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 \xd0\xba\xd3\xa9\xd0\xbf\xd1\x82\xd1\x96\xd0\xb3\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd \xd0\x91\xd2\x9a\xd0\xa5\xd2\x9a\xd0\x96 \xd1\x84\xd1\x83\xd0\xbd\xd0\xba\xd1\x86\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd \xd1\x81\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd1\x81\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f \xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb7\xd1\x96\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd\xd1\x96\xd2\xa3 \xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd \xd1\x81\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd2\x93\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd \xd1\x82\xd2\xb1\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd2\x9b\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b \xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb8\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82 \xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b (\xd1\x88\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd 150 \xd0\xb0\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbc).\n

\xd0\xa1\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd1\x83\xd2\x93\xd0\xb0 \xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd0\xba \xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0 \xd2\x9a\xd1\x8b\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9 \xd0\x9a\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbc\xd0\xbc\xd1\x83\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x96\xd0\xba \xd0\xbf\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd1\x82\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b \xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd \xd0\xa5\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd2\x9b\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 \xd1\x81\xd0\xb0\xd1\x8f\xd1\x81\xd0\xb8 \xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd2\xa3\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81 \xd0\xa1\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xba\xd1\x96\xd1\x80\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd \xd1\x81\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb3\xd1\x96\xd0\xb7 \xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xbe\xd0\xba\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd2\x9b \xd0\xbf\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd1\x82\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f \xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b\xd1\x81\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b.\n

\xd0\xae\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8c \xd3\x99\xd1\x83\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd1\x96 (1289 \xe2\x80\x93 1368) \xd0\xb4\xd3\x99\xd1\x83\xd1\x96\xd1\x80\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5 \xd2\x9b\xd1\x8b\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9 \xd0\xb4\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b \xd3\xa9\xd1\x80\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd \xd0\xb6\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b. \xd0\x96\xd0\xb0\xd2\xa3\xd0\xb0 \xd2\x9a\xd1\x8b\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9 \xd3\x99\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb1\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd\xd1\x96\xd2\xa3 \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb3\xd1\x96\xd0\xb7\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd \xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd1\x83\xd1\x88\xd1\x8b \xd0\x9b\xd1\x83 \xd0\xa1\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8c (1881 \xe2\x80\x93 1936) \xd0\xb1\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b. 1921 \xe2\x80\x93 22 \xd0\xb6\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b \xd1\x80\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb8\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x96\xd0\xba \xd0\xb6\xd3\x99\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5 \xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd1\x82\xd0\xb8\xd0\xba. \xd0\xb1\xd0\xb0\xd2\x93\xd1\x8b\xd1\x82\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd2\x93\xd1\x8b \xd3\x99\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb1\xd0\xb8 \xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbf\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80 \xd2\x9b\xd2\xb1\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b. \xd2\x9a\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb0\xd2\x9b \xd1\x82\xd1\x96\xd0\xbb\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xb1\xd1\x96\xd1\x80\xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80 \xd1\x88\xd1\x8b\xd2\x93\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b \xd0\xb0\xd1\x83\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbf, \xd0\xb6\xd0\xb5\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xba\xd1\x96\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbf \xd0\xb1\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbf \xd0\xb1\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b. \xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd1\x86\xd1\x8e\xd0\xb9 \xd0\xbf\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xb1\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b. 8 \xd2\x93\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b\xd1\x80\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 \xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0 \xd1\x88\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xa2\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd \xd0\xb8\xd0\xbc\xd0\xbf\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b \xd0\xa1\xd1\x8e\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8c-\xd1\x86\xd0\xb7\xd1\x83\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8c \xd1\x81\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 \xd0\xb6\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd \xd0\xbc\xd1\x83\xd0\xb7\xd1\x8b\xd0\xba\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd1\x82\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80 \xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd \xd0\xb1\xd0\xb8\xd1\x88\xd1\x96\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80, \xd3\x99\xd0\xbd\xd1\x88\xd1\x96\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80 \xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd \xc2\xab\xd0\x90\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbc\xd2\xb1\xd1\x80\xd1\x82 \xd0\xb1\xd0\xb0\xd2\x93\xd1\x8b\xc2\xbb (\xc2\xab\xd0\x9b\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8e\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8c\xc2\xbb) \xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b \xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd1\x80 \xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xba\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb1\xd1\x96 \xd2\x9b\xd2\xb1\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b. 17 \xe2\x80\x93 19 \xd2\x93\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b\xd1\x80\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xba\xd3\xa9\xd0\xbf\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd \xd0\xb6\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb3\xd1\x96\xd0\xbb\xd1\x96\xd0\xba\xd1\x82\xd1\x96 \xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd1\x80\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80: \xd0\xb1\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd1\x86\xd0\xb7\xd1\x8b, \xd1\x86\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8c-\xd1\x86\xd1\x8f\xd0\xbd, \xd1\x8e\xd1\x8d\xd1\x86\xd0\xb7\xd1\x8e\xd0\xb9, \xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd2\x93\xd1\x8b \xd0\xb1\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0 \xd2\x9b\xd2\xb1\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b.\n

19 \xd2\x93\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b\xd1\x80\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 \xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0 \xd1\x88\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xbe\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b \xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd1\x80\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80 \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb3\xd1\x96\xd0\xb7\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xbf\xd0\xb5\xd0\xba\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd1\x96\xd0\xba \xd0\xbc\xd1\x83\xd0\xb7. \xd0\xb4\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb0 (\xd1\x86\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbd\xd1\x81\xd0\xb8) \xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b \xd0\xb4\xd2\xaf\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x96. \xd2\x9a\xd1\x8b\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9 \xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb3\xd1\x96\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb3\xd1\x96 \xd1\x81\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbf\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b \xd0\xbe\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b \xd1\x86\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbd\xd1\x81\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0 \xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd2\x9b \xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbc\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd2\x93\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd.\n

\n\xd0\x9a\xd0\xbe\xd1\x82-\xd0\xb4\xe2\x80\x99\xd0\x98\xd0\xb2\xd1\x83\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80 \xe2\x80\xa2 \xd0\x9a\xd1\x83\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb9\xd1\x82 \xe2\x80\xa2 \xd0\x9f\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd1\x83 \xe2\x80\xa2 \xd0\x9f\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8c\xd1\x88\xd0\xb0 \xe2\x80\xa2 \xd0\xad\xd0\xba\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b\xd2\x9b \xd0\x93\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5\xd1\x8f

\xd0\x91\xd2\xb0\xd2\xb0 \xd0\xbc\xd2\xaf\xd1\x88\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81
